## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="e95ff-1598">Notes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e95ff-1598">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e95ff-1599">La classe **MS-DFSR-Subscriber** fait partie de la prise en charge du service de réplication système de fichiers DFS (DFS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e95ff-1599">The **ms-DFSR-Subscriber** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
